<script>
    (function() {
        window.onload = function () {
            var headerHeight = document.getElementById('wrapper-top').clientHeight;
            $( ".wrapper-outer" ).first().css( "margin-top", headerHeight + "px" );
        }
    })();

    function registerColorbox(){
        var root = window.location.protocol + '//' + window.location.host;
        var boxFix = (window.innerHeight > 950 ? true:false);
        $.colorbox({
            iframe:true,
            width:542,
            height:749,
            fixed: boxFix,
            scrolling: false,
            overlayClose: true,
            close: '<i class="hktvui sprite-common-overlay-close-22"></i>',
            href:function(){
                return root+'/hktv/zh/register';
            },
        });
    }

    window.addEventListener("message", receiveMessage, false);
    function receiveMessage(event)
    {
        if (event.origin.indexOf(window.location.host) == -1)
        return;

        if (event.data.indexOf('resize') != -1) {
            var elements = event.data.split(':');
            $.colorbox.resize({height:elements[1]});
        }
        else if (event.data == 'reload') {
            var sPageURL = parent.location.search.substring(1);
            var sURLVariables = sPageURL.split('&');
            var reloadFlag = true;
            var newSearch = '';
                for (var i = 0; i < sURLVariables.length; i++)
                {
                    if (i > 0)
                        newSearch += '&';

                    var sParameterName = sURLVariables[i].split('=');
                    if (sParameterName[0] == 'register' && sParameterName[1]=='true')
                    {
                        sParameterName[1] = 'false';
                        reloadFlag = false;
                    }
                    newSearch += sParameterName[0] + '=' + sParameterName[1];
                }


            if(reloadFlag) {
                location.reload(true);
            }
            else {
                location.replace(location.protocol + '//' + location.host + location.pathname + '?' + newSearch);
            }
        }
    }

</script>

        <script>
            var tempCategories = [];
            for (var kC in breadOrder.order){
                tempCategories.push(breadOrder.order[kC].categoryCode);
            }
            var zoneBanner = $(".hktv2015-all-catgories-container").zoneBanner({
                page: "homepage",
                lookup: false,
                zones: ["BA", "BB", "BC", "BD"],
                categories: tempCategories,
                lang: "zh"
            });

            
            $(document).on("breadRenderFinish", function(){
                /* create image div */
                if ($(".hktv-zone-m-bannerlist").length == 0){

                    $(".category-container").each(function(index){
                        var categoryCode = breadOrder.order[index]["categoryCode"];
                        $("<div class='hktv-zone-m-bannerlist' data-category='"+categoryCode+"'><div class='hktv-zone-ba' data-zone='BA' data-category='"+categoryCode+"'></div><div class='hktv-zone-bb' data-zone='BB' data-category='"+categoryCode+"'></div><div class='hktv-zone-bc' data-zone='BC' data-category='"+categoryCode+"'></div><div class='hktv-zone-bd' data-zone='BD' data-category='"+categoryCode+"'></div></div>").insertBefore(this);
                    });
                }
            });

            $(document).on('breadRenderFinishWithIndex', function(e, index){
                var scope = $(".hktv-zone-m-bannerlist").eq(index);
                zoneBanner.data("zoneBanner").fillBannersWithCategoryAndScope($(scope).data('category'),scope);
            });

        </script>
